,SANGS RGYAS SRAS DANG PHRAD GYUR CIG ,MCHOD PA'I SPRIN NI MTHA'
YAS PAS, ,'GRO BA'I BLA MA MCHOD PAR SHOG ,LHA YANG

 DUS SU CHAR 'BEBS SHING, ,LO TOG PHUN SUM TSOGS PAR SHOG ,RGYAL
PO CHOS BZHIN BYED GYUR CIG ,'JIG RTEN DAG KYANG DAR BAR SHOG
,SMAN RNAMS MTHU DANG LDAN PA DANG, ,GSANG SNGAGS BZLAS BRJOD
GRUB PAR SHOG ,MKHA' 'GRO

SRIN PO LA SOGS PA, ,SNYING RJE'I SEMS DANG LDAN GYUR CIG ,SEMS
CAN 'GA' YANG SDUG MA GYUR, ` ,SDIG PAR MA GYUR NAM GYUR, ('DIS
BZANG BA'I 'GREL PA LAS BYUNG,) 'JIG DANG BRNYAS PAR MI 'GYUR
ZHING, ,'GA' YANG YID MI BDE MA GYUR,,

GTZUG LAG KHANG RNAMS KLOG PA DANG, ,KHA TON GYIS RGYAS LEGS
GNAS SHOG ,RTAG TU DGE 'DUN MTHUN PA DANG, ,DGE 'DUN DON YANG
'GRUB PAR SHOG ,BSLAB PA 'DOD PA'I DGE SLONG DAG ,DBEN PA DAG
KYANG THOB PAR SHOG ,G-YENG

PA THAMS CAD SPANGS NAS NI, ,SEMS NI LAS RUNG BSGOM GYUR CIG
,DGE SLONG MA RNAMS RNYED LDAN ZHING, ,'THAB DANG GNOD PA SPANGS
BAR SHOG ,DE BZHIN RAB TU BYUNG BA KUN, ,TSUL KHRIMS NYAMS PA
MED GYUR CIG ,TSUL KHRIMS 'TSAL

BAS YID BYUNG NAS, ,RTAG TU SDIG PA ZAD BYED SHOG ,BDE 'GRO DAG
KYANG THOB GYUR NAS, ,DER YANG BRTUL ZHUGS MI NYAMS SHOG ,MKHAS
PA RNAMS NI BKUR BA DANG, ,BSOD SNYOMS DAG KYANG RNYED PAR
SHOG ,RGYUD NI YONGS SU DAG

@081A *, ,PA DANG, ,PHYOGS RNAMS KUN TU GRAGS PAR SHOG ,NGAN
SONG SDUG BSNGAL MI MYONG ZHING, ,DKA' BA SPYAD PA MED PAR YANG,
,LHA BAS LHAG PA'I LUS KYIS NI, ,DE DAG SANGS RGYAS MYUR 'GRUB
SHOG ,

SEMS CAN KUN GYIS LAN MANG DU, ,SANGS RGYAS THAMS CAD MCHOD BYED
CING, ,SANGS RGYAS BDE BA BSAM YAS KYIS, ,RTAG TU BDE DANG LDAN
GYUR CIG ` (,'JIG RTEN LAS 'DAS PA'I DON DU BSNGO BA,) BYANG
CHUB SEMS DPA' RNAMS KYIS NI, ,'GRO

@082A *, (,GNYIS GYI BSTAN PA'I BDAG PO, RNGO BO AA TI SHA DANG
ZHAL MI GNYIS PA'I NGES PA DON GYI BSHES GNYEN MTSUNGS ZLA MA
MCHIS PA, KHYAB BDAG 'KHOR LO'I MGON PO RJE PHA BONG KHA PA BDE
CHEN SNYING PO DPAL BZANG PO MCHOG NAS, ME BYI LOR MDO KHAMS
CHAB MDO DGE LDAN BYAMS PA GLING DU 'DI'I BSHAD

MDZAD BREL SHIN TU 'DZINGS CHE'I SENG BAR DU GONG GSAL BKA'
MCHAN THOR BU 'DI DAG PHYAG BSTAR MAR DGYES STZAL THOG ,DA DUNG
'DI LA ZHU DAG ZHIB TSA MDZAD DGOS MANG DU YOD TSUL YANG YANG
PHEBS KYANG, PHYIS CHOS 'KHOR RGYA CHE GZHAN MANG POS GO SKABS
'PHROGS TE LJAGS ZHU SPYAN BSTAR ZHU
